24 accessory buildings and uses customarily incident to the above uses b parking regulations where any building or structure is erected reconstructed or converted for any of the business or commercial purposes or uses permitted in this section parking spaces shall be provided in the ratio of not less than one parking space for each 1000 square feet or fraction thereof in the ground floor of said building which is used for commercial purposes such parking space may be located on the same lot as the building or on an area within 300 feet of the building two or more owners of buildings may join together in providing such parking space c erection of signs signs shall be permitted in this district and shall be erected in such a manner as to be completely and entirely supported at or in rear of the approved front building line and extend no more than ten feet forward of that line and no less than eight feet above the grade at the building line and no nearer than two feet to a line perpendicular to the outside curbline of the street  1 c industrial regulations the regulations set forth in this section or set forth elsewhere in this ordinance when referred to in this section are the district regulations for the c industrial district a use regulations a building or premises may be used for any purpose whatsoever not in conflict with any ordinance of the city of canton including this ordinance except that no lot premises or building shall be used for and no building or occupancy permit shall be issued for residential purposes unless the same shall conform and comply in all respects to the residential regulations including use regulations area regulations intensity of use and parking regulations applicable to the nearest residential use district  and except that no lot premises or building shall be used for and no building or occupancy permit shall be issued for any of the following uses unless the location of such use shall have been approved by the mayor and board of aldermen after report by the building official 1 abattoirs 2 acid manufacture 3 cement lime gypsum or plaster of paris manufacture 4 chemical manufacture 5 cotton gins 6 distillation of bones 7 explosives manufacture or storage 8 fat rendering 9 fertilizer manufacture 10 garbage offal or dead animals reduction or dumping 11 gas manufacture or storage 12 glue size or gelatin manufacture 13 junkyards or storage of used automobile bodies or parts 14 paper or pulp manufacture 15 petroleum refining 16 sawmills 17 stockyards stock auction barns or slaughter of animals or poultry 18 tannery 19 wholesale storage of gasoline or other inflammable materials 20 in general those uses which have been or may hereafter be declared a nuisance by any court of record  or which may be noxious or offensive or dangerous to public health or safety by reason of odor dust smoke gas fumes noise vibration or excessive lights b parking regulations 1 where any building or structure is erected reconstructed or converted for any of the uses permitted in this section parking spaces shall be provided in the ratio of not less than one parking space for each 1000 square feet or fraction thereof in the building 2 in addition to the parking regulations hereinbefore prescribed in this ordinance there shall be provided for any business commercial or industrial use permitted in the b commercial district or the c industrial district offstreet facilities for the loading and unloading of merchandise and goods in such a manner as not to obstruct traffic upon any public street  2 nonconforming uses 1 the lawful use of any building or premises existing at the time of the passage of this ordinance may be continued although such use does not conform to the provisions hereof if no structural alterations are made a nonconforming use of a building may be changed to another nonconforming use of the same or of a more restricted classification whenever a nonconforming use has been changed to a more restricted use or to a conforming use such use shall not thereafter be changed to a less restricted use 2 whenever the use of a building or premises becomes nonconforming change in the zoning ordinance or district boundaries such use may be continued  and if no structural alterations are made it may be changed to another nonconforming use of the same or of a more restricted classification 3 in the event that a nonconforming use of any building or premises is discontinued or its normal operation stopped the use of same shall thereafter conform to the uses permitted in the district in which it is located 4 when a building the use of which does not conform to the provisions of this ordinance is damaged by fire explosion act of god or the public enemy to the extent of more than 50 percent of its fair market value it shall not be restored except in conformity with the district regulations of the district in which the building is located building and occupancy permits 1 building permits shall first be obtained from the building official as required by section 4 of the building code of the city of canton 2 certificates of occupancy shall be applied for coincidentally with the application for a building permit on forms to be prescribed and furnished by the building official and shall be issued within ten days after the lawful erection or alteration of the building is completed a record of all such certificates shall be kept on file in the office of the city clerk and copies shall be furnished on request to any person having a proprietary or tenancy interest in the building affected upon payment of a fee of $050 therefor 3 no lot shall be occupied or used and no building hereafter erected or structurally altered shall be occupied or used in whole or in part for any purpose whatsoever until a certificate of occupancy is issued by the building official stating that the building or premises and the use thereof comply with the provisions of this ordinance the building code and all other ordinances of the city of canton 4 no change of use shall be made in any building or part thereof now existing or hereafter erected or structurally altered without a permit being issued therefor by the building official and no permit shall be issued to make any such change in use unless the change is in conformity with the provisions of this ordinance 5 no permit for excavation or the erection or structural alteration of any building shall be issued before the application has been made for a certificate of occupancy and no building or premises shall be occupied until such certificate and permit are issued appeals and petitions the mayor and board of aldermen shall hear and decide appeals from any order requirement decision or determination of the building official in the administration and enforcement of this ordinance  and shall also hear and decide all petitions for exceptions and variations as hereinafter authorized appeals may be taken by any person aggrieved or affected by any decision of the building official such appeal shall be taken within two weeks after the date of the commission of the act complained of by filing with the building official a notice of appeal specifying the grounds thereof  and said building official shall forthwith transmit to the city clerk all of the papers constituting the record upon which the action appealed from was taken the city clerk shall immediately notify the mayor who shall fix a time and place for the hearing of such appeal and shall issue a call therefor and the city clerk shall give public notice of the hearing of such appeal by publishing a notice to all interested persons one time at least 15 days prior to the date fixed for the hearing of appeal in a newspaper of general circulation published in the municipality at the hearing any party may appear in person or by agent or by attorney petitions for exceptions or variations may be filed with the city clerk and hearing shall be had thereon in the same manner and after the same notice as hereinabove provided for appeals exceptions and variations a upon the hearing of any petition or appeal the mayor and board of aldermen may permit the following exceptions or variations 1 where the strict application of this ordinance would result in peculiar and exceptional practical difficulties or to exceptional hardship upon the owner of such property the board may authorize a variation from such strict application so as to relieve such difficulties or hardships as for example by reason of exceptional narrowness shallowness or shape of a specific piece of property existing at the time of the original adoption of this ordinance or by reason of exceptional topographical conditions or other extraordinary or exceptional situation or condition of a specific piece of property or by reason of the location of trees natural drainage courses lakes or other desirable features which condition is not generally prevalent in the neighborhood 2 to permit the extension of a use district where the boundary line of a district divides a lot or parcel of land in single ownership as shown of record as of the date of the passage of this ordinance 3 to permit the erection and use of a building or use of premises in any location for a public service corporation for public utility purposes which the board deems reasonably necessary for the public convenience or welfare 4 to interpret the provisions of this ordinance where the street layout actually on the ground varies from the street layout as shown on the map fixing the several districts which map is attached to and made a part of this ordinance 5 to vary the parking regulations of this ordinance whenever the character or use of a building is such as to make unnecessary the full provision of parking facilities or where such regulations would impose an unreasonable hardship upon the use of the lot as contrasted with merely granting an advantage or a convenience b in the consideration of all such appeals and petitions the board shall before making any finding or decision or permitting any exception or variation first determine that the proposed decision exception or variation will not constitute a change in the zoning map or use districts and will not impair an adequate supply of light and air to adjacent property or impair established property values within the surrounding area or in any other respect impair the health safety comfort morals or welfare of the city of canton every decision on appeal and every exception or variation granted or denied shall be accompanied by a written finding of fact specifying the reasons therefor in the event of a protest against any change or variation signed by the owners of 20 percent or more either of the area of the lots included in the proposed exception or variation or of those immediately adjacent to the rear thereof extending 160 feet therefrom or of those directly opposite thereto extending 160 feet from the street frontage of such opposite lots such exception or variation shall not become effective except by the favorable vote of twothirds  23  of the elected membership of the board amendments the mayor and board of aldermen may from time to time on their own motion or on petition after public notice given as in case of the adoption of this ordinance amend the regulations and districts herein established  but no such amendment shall become effective until after a public hearing in relation thereto at which parties in interest and citizens shall have an opportunity to be heard after at least 15 days notice of the time and place of such hearing shall have been published in a newspaper of general circulation in the city of canton in case of a protest against such amendment signed by the owners of 20 percent or more either of the area of the lots included in such proposed change or of those immediately adjacent to the rear thereof extending 160 feet therefrom or of those directly opposite thereto extending 160 feet from the street frontage of such opposite lots such amendment shall not become effective except by the favorable vote of twothirds of all of the members of the board of aldermen of the city of canton prior to the setting of a date for public hearing of any petition for exception variation or amendment to this ordinance the applicant for the proposed exception variation or amendment shall deposit with the city clerk the estimated cost of the necessary publication payable to the account of the city of canton interpretation purpose and conflict in interpreting and applying this ordinance its provisions shall be held to be the minimum requirements for the promotion of the public safety health convenience comfort morals prosperity and general welfare it is not intended by this ordinance to interfere with or abrogate or annul any ordinance rules regulations or permits previously adopted or issued and not in conflict with any of the provisions of this ordinance or which shall be adopted or issued pursuant to law relating to the use of building or premises and likewise not in conflict with this ordinance  nor is it intended by this ordinance to interfere with or abrogate or annul any easements covenants or other agreements between parties except that if this ordinance imposes a greater restriction this ordinance shall control violation penalty and enforcement a any person firm or corporation who shall violate any of the provisions of this ordinance or fail to comply therewith or with any of the requirements thereof or who shall build or alter any building in violation of any detailed statement or plan submitted and approved hereunder shall be deemed guilty of a misdemeanor and shall upon conviction be punished by a fine of not less than $500 or more than $10000 or by imprisonment in the city jail for not more than 30 days or by both such fine and imprisonment  and each day such violation shall be permitted to exist shall be and constitute a separate offense and may be punished as such the owner or owners of any building or premises or part thereof where anything in violation of this ordinance shall be placed or shall exist and any architect builder contractor individual person or corporation employed in connection therewith and who may have assisted in the commission of any such violation shall be deemed guilty of a separate offense and upon conviction shall be punished as herein provided b in case any building or structure is erected constructed reconstructed altered repaired converted or maintained or any building structure or land is used in violation of this ordinance the building official in addition to other remedies may institute any appropriate action or proceedings in the name of the city of canton madison county mississippi to prevent such unlawful erection construction reconstruction alteration repair conversion maintenance or use to restrain correct or abate such violation to prevent the occupancy of said building structure or land or to prevent any illegal act conduct business or use in or about said premises validity should any section or provision of this ordinance be declared by a court of competent jurisdiction to be invalid that decision shall not affect the validity of the ordinance as a whole or any part thereof other than the part so declared to be invalid this board hereby declaring that it would have adopted those parts of this ordinance which are valid and omitted any parts which may be unconstitutional or otherwise invalid if it had known that such part or parts were invalid at the time of the adoption of this ordinance repealing clause all ordinances or parts of ordinances inconsistent and in conflict herewith are hereby repealed effective date this ordinance shall take effect and be in force after its final passage and publication according to law  however no such regulation restriction or boundary shall become effective until after a public hearing in relation thereto at which parties in interest and citizens shall have an opportunity to be heard in accordance with law notice of intention to adopt that in order for all interested parties and citizens to have an opportunity to be heard and to have full notice of this comprehensive zoning plan including the said map and the regulations and restrictions set forth herein the city clerk of the city of canton be and she hereby is directed to give notice to property owners parties in interest and citizens of the city of canton madison county mississippi by publication of this ordinance at least once in the madison county herald a newspaper of general circulation in said city that on tuesday the seventh day of october 195 the mayor and board of aldermen of the city of canton madison county mississippi will meet at the city hall in said city at  oclock pm for the purpose of hearing any and all objections and protests with reference to the use districts or boundaries thereof as well as to any and all terms and provisions of this proposed zoning ordinance such interested parties are further given notice that the said use district or zoning map is on file in the office of the city clerk of said city of canton and is open for inspection by anyone desiring to examine same any property owner parties in interest and citizens who may be aggrieved with any of the terms and provisions hereof including information disclosed by an examination of said map may present their objections and protests in writing to the said city clerk at her office in the city hall in canton mississippi on or before said date or may appear in person or by attorney and present the same before the said mayor and board of aldermen at the said hearing after such objections and protests as may be presented have been heard and disposed of such changes and corrections made as the mayor and board may determine this ordinance will be made final and shall be in force and effect according to law adopted at this the regular september meeting of the mayor and board of aldermen held on tuesday the second day of september 1958 s percy f parke mayor attest s bertha mckay clerk seal
